Ferrari is an Italian luxury sports car manufacturer, renowned worldwide for its high-performance vehicles, distinctive design, and strong racing heritage. Founded in 1939 by Enzo Ferrari in Maranello, Italy, the brand symbolizes speed, innovation, and exclusivity.
Luxury/Marketing Style: Ferrari represents the ultimate fusion of art, engineering, and passion. Every model embodies cutting-edge technology, Italian craftsmanship, and iconic styling, making Ferrari not just a car, but a lifestyle and a status symbol.
Automotive/Technical Style: Ferrari produces high-performance sports cars and supercars powered by advanced engines, precise aerodynamics, and innovative design. Known for their distinctive &ldquo;Prancing Horse&rdquo; logo and unmatched Formula 1 legacy, Ferraris deliver exceptional speed, handling, and driving experience.
Ferrari

Kalaat el-Andalous
detail
At&nbsp;ELITE MOTORS&nbsp;we believe that customers are our biggest asset. Adopting customer-centric mindset, it became a culture at our company to provide state of the art customer experience. With many years of experience in automotive field,&nbsp;Elite Motors&nbsp;a renamed company in Qatar is proud to present you&nbsp;CHERY&nbsp;high standard vehicles and its facilities in Qatar.

https://www.kia.com/fr/modeles/picanto/fiche-technique/Comme leur nom lindique, les citadines sont destin&eacute;es &agrave; un usage majoritairement urbain. Pour se faufiler, elles sont de petite taille. Cette cat&eacute;gorie se segmente en deux : dun c&ocirc;t&eacute; les minicitadines (type Renault Twingo ou Peugeot 108), vraiment courtes, de lautre les polyvalentes (type Peugeot 208 ou Dacia Sandero), un peu plus grandes. Voici les meilleures sur le march&eacute; de la seconde main.
